<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:знаменательный.html>знамена́тельный</a> (17256)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знаменовать.html>знаменова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">znamenovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знаменательный.html>знамена́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">znamenátelʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)знамена́тельнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)знамена́тельней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>significant, remarkable, noteworthy, portentous, momentous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:знаменательный.html>знамена́тельное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:событие.html>собы́тие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>znamenátelʹnoje</b> sobýtije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">important/momentous event</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">linguistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> categorematic, significant
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:знаменательный.html>знамена́тельные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>znamenátelʹnyje</b> slova</i> ― <span class="e-translation">categorematic words</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***знаменитый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:знаменитый.html>знамени́тый</a> (1139)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*znamę</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sign</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знаменитый.html>знамени́тый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">znamenítyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>famous, renowned, celebrated, noted, notorious, distinguished, eminent, illustrious
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:парк.html>парк</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:знаменитый.html>знамени́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:статуя.html>ста́туями</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Étot park <b>znamenít</b> svoími státujami.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This park <b>is famous</b> for its statues.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:знание.html>зна́ние</a> (1121)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">znatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знание.html>зна́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">znánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знание.html>зна́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знание.html>зна́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знание.html>зна́ний</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">znatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знаток.html>знато́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">znatók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знаток.html>знатока́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знаток.html>знатоки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знаток.html>знатоко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cognoscente, connoisseur, pundit, adept, maven, expert</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>зна<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ток.html>то́к</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3b  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-зна-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-т-ок</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***знать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a> (569)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ти</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">znati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*znati</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*źnōˀtei</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵnéh₃t</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵneh₃-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">know</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cunning</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">canny</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">notice</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">gnostic</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">znatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:узнать.html>узна́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to know: to be familiar with or accustomed to a person, place, or thing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ю</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja jejó xorošó <b>znáju</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I <b>know</b> her well.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ю</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:математика.html>матема́тику</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja xorošó <b>znáju</b> matemátiku.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I <b>know</b> math well.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to know: to be in possession of a specific fact or datum
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ю</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>живёт</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>znáju</b>, gde on živjót.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I <b>know</b> where he lives.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ю</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плюс.html>плюс</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>znáju</b>, skólʹko dva pljus dva.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I <b>know</b> how much two plus two is.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ю</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja ne <b>znáju</b>, kogdá éto býlo.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I don’t <b>know</b> when it was.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">znatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ти</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">collective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nobility, noble people</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">nobility</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аристократия.html>аристокра́тия</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">aristokrátija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высший.html>вы́сшее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:общество.html>о́бщество</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výsšeje óbščestvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:элита.html>эли́та</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">elíta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> it seems, then</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знахарь.html>зна́харь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">znáxarʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знахарь.html>зна́харя</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знахарь.html>зна́хари</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знахарь.html>зна́харей</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">знаха́рка</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зна́харка</b>)

***значение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a> (1076)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:значить.html>зна́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">znáčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">značénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>significance, meaning, sense
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двоякий.html>двоя́кое</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dvojákoje <b>značénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">double <b>meaning</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:автор.html>а́втор</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:придать.html>прида́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любимый.html>люби́мому</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:герой.html>геро́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:символический.html>символи́ческое</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ávtor pridál svojemú ljubímomu geróju simvolíčeskoje <b>značénije</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The author attached a symbolic <b>meaning</b> to his favorite character.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>significance, importance, consequence, weight</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:значительный.html>значи́тельный</a> (1809)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:значить.html>зна́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">znáčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:значительный.html>значи́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">značítelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>considerable, sizeable, strong, substantial, large</li>
<li>important, consequential, significant</li>
<li>meaningful, suggestive</li></ol>

***значить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:значить.html>зна́чить</a> (195)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>знак</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">znak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:значить.html>зна́чить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">znáčitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to mean, to signify
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>Что</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:значить.html>зна́чит</a></b> XX?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Što <b>znáčit</b> XX?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What does XX <b>mean</b>?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to mean, to be of importance, to matter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:значить.html>зна́чит</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná dlja menjá mnógo <b>znáčit</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She <b>means</b> a lot to me.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:знойный.html>зно́йный</a> (12256)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зной.html>зной</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">znoj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знойный.html>зно́йный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">znójnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>scorching, hot, sultry</li>
<li>passionate, hot</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:зной.html>зно́й</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-зной-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***зов.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зов.html>зов</a> (11327)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="None mention" lang="ru">-∅</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-∅</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зов.html>зов</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zov</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зов.html>зо́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зов.html>зо́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зов.html>зо́вов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>call, summons
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>прийти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвому</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зо́ву</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prijtí po pérvomu <b>zóvu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to come at the first summons</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откликнуться.html>откли́кнуться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зов.html>зов</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otklíknutʹsja na <b>zov</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to respond to the call/summons, to answer a summons</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
